# GERMAN ID-Based Rejected Credit Decisions

Each rejected application receives three different actionable decisions.

## german_000001 / Decision 1

- Decision: Reduce requested loan amount
- Original probability of good credit: `0.3631`
- Probability after decision: `0.3943`
- Decision threshold: `0.3900`
- Would approve after this decision: `True`

Customer-facing recommendation:
- Requested loan amount could be reduced from 5951.0 to about 4463.0.
- Installment burden could be lowered from 2.0 to about 1.0, for example with more income, a lower amount, or a down payment.
